        云游凤凰古城 赏别样民俗风情
       </span>
       <span class="brief">
        享有“北平遥，南凤凰”之名，青石板街道、沱江边的吊脚楼、古建筑以及浓厚的苗族风情，构成了独具一格的湘西韵味。
       </span>
      </a>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="pic">
     <img class="lazy" data-echo="//p4.img.cctvpic.com/photoAlbum/page/performance/img/2021/3/2/1614672070831_329.jpg" src="//p1.img.cctvpic.com/photoAlbum/templet/common/DEPA1546583592748817/Bottomplan.gif"/>
     <div class="pic_num">
      <div class="pic_numBg">
       <span>
        慢享哈尔滨都市风光
       </span>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="pic_con">
      <span class="icon">
       正在直播
      </span>
      <a class="txt" href="https://livechina.cctv.com/zbdcy/index.shtml?spm=0.PiHRJ12Bw7m4.EHitFunzldUG.29&amp;pageID=PAGEdJvWXtRSRLGS4rHarVf3201124&amp;interactionId=INTEjFy3QjZXqVw2M5XfMafy201120" target="_blank">
       <span class="title">
        到霁虹桥打卡梦幻冰城哈尔滨
       </span>
       <span class="brief">
        霁虹桥建成于1926年，是哈尔滨的重要交通枢纽。霁虹桥见证了哈尔滨发展的历史，成为一代代哈尔滨人心中的寄托。
       </span>
      </a>

   Echo.init({

function get_cntv_whereis(cntv_whereis){
	var chunwan_areaInfo = eval('(' + cntv_whereis.replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g, "") + ')');
	country_code = chunwan_areaInfo.country_code;
	//video_player_box();
	setCookie_tvzhibo("country_code",country_code);
	}
function setCookie_tvzhibo(name, value) {
		var Days = 0.25;
		var exp = new Date();
		exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
		document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + ";expires=" + exp.toGMTString()
	}

CCTV_2020ad.prototype._ajax = function(url,cb,fn){
    $.ajax({
        url:url,
        dataType:"jsonp",
        jsonpCallback:cb,
        success:function(data){
            fn(data);
        }
    })
}

        $("#gtyb_jh").html('<div class="jhbox '+date_move+'" style="position:absolute;top: 0;"><a target="_blank" href="'+ba+'"><img class="" style="width:100%;" src="'+bsrc+'"></a><div class="" style="position: absolute; left: 0px; bottom: 0px; z-index: 999; padding: 0px 3px; font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(0, 0, 0) none repeat scroll 0% 0%; opacity: 0.5;">广告</div></div>');
